| 1:05:15| or whether it is, in fact, replaced by a new teacher.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoComWSR1467181113?start=3915)|

| 1:05:24| you're looking at gaining $12,000 to $15,000 per position that retires.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoComWSR1467181113?start=3924)|
| 1:05:30| Obviously, if it's lost through attrition, you're losing the full dollar value of that position.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoComWSR1467181113?start=3930)|
| 1:05:37| The second part of that is for every new hire that you have that replaces someone that retires right now.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoComWSR1467181113?start=3937)|
| 1:05:43| Most of you all are aware of our TCRS legacy plan.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoComWSR1467181113?start=3943)|
| 1:05:47| Our employer contribution to that is 10.46% for every teacher.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoComWSR1467181113?start=3947)|
